9.2 C language level POSIX interface

Several files are involved in the full implementation of the POSIX interface: 

     src/ikarus-posix.c
     lib/vicare/unsafe-capi.sls
     scheme/ikarus.posix.sls
     scheme/makefile.sps
     tests/test-vicare-posix.sps

File pathnames are bytevectors at the C language level and strings at the Scheme language level; the conversion is performed with the function in the parameter string->filename-func.

The authoritative documentation for all the interface functions is the one of the C library on the platform's operating system; this file gives only a brief overview of the features and explains the Scheme adaptation.

  • capi posix adding: How to add a POSIX primitive.
  • capi posix errno: Handling errno codes.
  • capi posix env: Operating system environment variables.
  • capi posix port: File descriptors and Scheme ports.
  • capi posix pid: Process identifier functions.
  • capi posix process: Forking and executing processes.
  • capi posix status: Process termination status.
  • capi posix signals: Delivering interprocess signals.
  • capi posix stat: File system inspection.
  • capi posix file: File system interface.
  • capi posix link: Hard and symbolic links.
  • capi posix dir: File system directories.
  • capi posix fd: File descriptors at low level.
  • capi posix socket: Network sockets.
  • capi posix users: Users and groups.
  • capi posix job: Job control.
  • capi posix time: Time and date.

Next: capi posix errno, Up: capi posix

9.2.1 How to add a POSIX primitive

We must remember that the POSIX primitives end up exported by both the (vicare) and (ikarus) libraries; following the example of the getpid() function, to add a POSIX primitive we should follow these steps:

  1. In the file src/ikarus-posix.c add the primitive C language function: 
              ikptr
          ikrt_posix_getpid(void)
          {
            int   retval = getpid();
            return fix(retval);
          }
  2. In the file lib/vicare/unsafe-capi.sls add the following macro definition to the library: 
              (define-inline (posix-getpid)
            (foreign-call "ikrt_posix_getpid"))

    and add the binding to the export list.

  3. In the file scheme/ikarus.posix.sls: add the binding to both the export list of the library and to the except import list from (ikarus); add the function implementation calling a syntax associated to the foreign function: 
              (define (getpid)
            (posix-getpid))
  4. In the file scheme/makefile.sps: add an entry for the function to the list bound to identifier->library-map to have the function exported by (ikarus) and (vicare): 
              (getpid         i v)
  5. In the file tests/test-vicare-posix.sps add test cases for the function.

Next: capi posix env, Previous: capi posix adding, Up: capi posix

9.2.2 Handling errno codes

Vicare makes use of the platform's own errno codes; they are negated to make them different from file descriptors, and so distinguishable when used as single return values from C functions, and converted to fixnums. Example: if the C language code for EPERM is the integer 1, the corresponding Scheme language value is the fixnum -1.

— Function: ikptr ik_errno_to_code (void)

Negate the current errno value and convert the result into a fixnum, return the fixnum. When an error occurs: many functions call this function and return its return value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_strerror (ikptr ec, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function strerror(), strerror. Convert a fixnum representing an encoded errno code into a bytevector holding the string message which describes it; return a reference to the bytevector; if ec is invalid: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_last_errno (ikpcb * pcb)

Return a fixnum representing the negated value of errno right after the last call to a foreign function through the FFI.

Next: capi posix port, Previous: capi posix errno, Up: capi posix

9.2.3 Accessing environment variables

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getenv (ikptr variable, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getenv(), getenv. Retrieve the value of environment variables. variable must reference a bytevector object representing the name of the environment variable. If the environment variable is set: return a bytevector representing its value; else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setenv (ikptr variable, ikptr value, ikptr overwrite)

Interface to the C function setenv(), setenv. Set a new value for an environment variable.

variable must reference a bytevector object representing the name of the environment variable; value must reference a bytevector object representing the new value. If overwrite is false_object and the environment variable already exists: the environment variable is left untouched; else the new value is set, either creating a new environment variable or replacing the old value.

If successful return true_object; if an error occurs in setenv() return false_object.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_unsetenv (ikptr variable)

Interface to the C function unsetenv(), unsetenv. Unset an environment variable. variable must reference a bytevector object representing the name of the environment variable. Return true if variable has the correct format, else return false; there is no way to know if a variable was actually unset.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_environ (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the global C variable environ, unsetenv. Retrieve the full environment. Return a list of bytevectors representing the contents of the environ array; if the environment is empty (no environment variables set) return nil.

Next: capi posix pid, Previous: capi posix env, Up: capi posix

9.2.4 File descriptors and Scheme ports

  • capi posix port open: Opening and closing file descriptors.
  • capi posix port seek: Handling file descriptor cursor.
  • capi posix port rw: Reading and writing.
  • capi posix port event: Handling file descriptor events.
  • capi posix port net: Handling sockets.

Next: capi posix port seek, Up: capi posix port
9.2.4.1 Opening and closing file descriptors
— Function: ikptr ikrt_close_fd (ikptr fd)

Interface to the close() C function. close. Close a file descriptor.

fd must be a fixnum representing a file descriptor.

If successful return false_object; if an error occurs in close() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_open_input_fd (ikptr pathname)

Interface to the open() C function. open. Open a file for reading, using open mode O_RDONLY.

pathname must reference a bytevector object holding the file pathname.

If successful return a fixnum representing the file descriptor; if an error occurs in open() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_open_output_fd (ikptr pathname, ikptr opts)

Interface to the open() C function. open. Open a file for writing with configurable mode based on O_WRONLY; the access permissions when a new file is created are S_IRUSR | S_IWUSR | S_IRGRP | S_IROTH.

pathname must reference a bytevector object holding the file pathname; opts must be a fixnum with the following encoding:

0
The open mode is O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_EXCL.
1
The open mode is O_WRONLY | O_TRUNC.
2
The open mode is O_WRONLY | O_TRUNC | O_CREAT.
3
The open mode is O_WRONLY | O_TRUNC.
4
The open mode is O_WRONLY | O_CREAT | O_EXCL.
5
The open mode is O_WRONLY | O_CREAT.
6
The open mode is O_WRONLY | O_CREAT.
7
The open mode is O_WRONLY.

If successful return a fixnum representing the file descriptor; if an error occurs in open() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_open_input_output_fd (ikptr pathname, ikptr opts)

Interface to the open() C function. open. Open a file for reading and writing with configurable mode based on O_RDWR; the access permissions when a new file is created are S_IRUSR | S_IWUSR | S_IRGRP | S_IROTH.

pathname must reference a bytevector object holding the file pathname; opts must be a fixnum representing the opening flags, it has the same format of the opts argument to ikrt_open_output_fd.

If successful return a fixnum representing the file descriptor; if an error occurs in open() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

Next: capi posix port rw, Previous: capi posix port open, Up: capi posix port
9.2.4.2 Handling file descriptor cursor
— Function: ikptr ikrt_set_position (ikptr fd, ikptr pos)

Interface to the lseek() C function. lseek. Set the cursor position.

fd must be a fixnum representing a file descriptor; pos must be an exact integer in the range of the off_t platform type.

If successful return false_object; if an error occurs in lseek() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

Next: capi posix port event, Previous: capi posix port seek, Up: capi posix port
9.2.4.3 Reading and writing
— Function: ikptr ikrt_read_fd (ikptr fd, ikptr buffer, ikptr buffer-start, ikptr size)

Interface to the read() C function. read. Read data from a file descriptor.

fd must be a fixnum representing a file descriptor; buffer must reference a bytevector object in which the data will be stored; buffer-start must be a fixnum representing the offset in the buffer at which data will be written; size must be a fixnum representing the number of bytes to read.

If successful return a fixnum representing the number of bytes actually read and stored in the buffer; if an error occurs in read() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_write_fd (ikptr fd, ikptr buffer, ikptr buffer-start, ikptr size)

Interface to the write() C function. write. Write data to a file descriptor.

fd must be a fixnum representing a file descriptor; buffer must reference a bytevector object from which the data will be read; buffer-start must be a fixnum representing the offset in the buffer from which data will be read; size must be a fixnum representing the number of bytes to write.

If successful return a fixnum representing the number of bytes actually written; if an error occurs in write() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

Next: capi posix port net, Previous: capi posix port rw, Up: capi posix port
9.2.4.4 Handling file descriptor events
— Function: ikptr ikrt_select (ikptr max-fd, ikptr rfds, ikptr wfds, ikptr xfds)

Interface to the select() C function. select. Poll for events on sets of file descriptors, without timeout.

max-fd must be a fixnum representing the maximum file descriptor for which to wait for events; rfds, wfds and xfds must reference bytevectors holding fd_set data structures.

If successful return a fixnum representing the return value from select(); if an error occurs in select() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code(). Notice that if the call is interrupted by a signal, so it returns with EINTR, the function returns with error without reattempting the call.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_make_fd_nonblocking (ikptr fd)

Interface to the fcntl() C function. fcntl. Set non–blocking mode for a file descriptor.

fd must be a fixnum representing the file descriptor.

If successful return the raw C language NULL pointer; if an error occurs in fcntl() return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

Previous: capi posix port event, Up: capi posix port
9.2.4.5 Handling sockets
— Function: ikptr ikrt_tcp_connect (ikptr host, ikptr srvc)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_ucp_connect (ikptr host, ikptr srvc)

Interface to the getaddrinfo(), socket() and connect() C functions. Sockets. Establish a client connection to a remote server using the SOCK_STREAM or SOCK_DGRAM style.

host must reference a bytevector holding the remote server hostname; srvc must reference a bytevector holding the service specification.

If successful return a fixnum representing the socket; if an error occurs resolving the host name and address, return false_object; if an error occurs in one of the C function calls, return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_listen (ikptr port-number)

Interface to the socket(), bind(), listen() and setsockopt() C functions. Sockets. Create a server socket bound to the given port number for the local host, using the AF_INET namespace and the SOCK_STREAM style; the option SO_REUSEADDR is set for the server socket; at most 1024 concurrent connections to the socket will be enqueued.

port-number must be a fixnum representing the port number to use.

If successful return a fixnum representing the server socket; if an error occurs in one of the C function calls, return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_accept (ikptr sock, ikptr sockaddr)

Interface to the accept() C function. accept. Accept a connection to a server socket.

sock must be a fixnum representing the server socket; sockaddr must reference a bytevector object which will hold the struct sockaddr describing the client's address.

If successful return a fixnum representing the client socket and fill sockaddr with the client address; if an error occurs in accept(), return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_shutdown (ikptr sock)

Interface to the shutdown() C function. shutdown. Close a socket for both reading and writing.

sock must be a fixnum representing the socket.

If successful return the raw C language NULL pointer; if an error occurs in shutdown(), return the return value of ik_errno_to_code().

Next: capi posix process, Previous: capi posix port, Up: capi posix

9.2.5 Process identifier functions

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getpid (void)

Return the process identifier as fixnum. getpid.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getppid (void)

Return the parent process identifier as fixnum. getpid.

Next: capi posix status, Previous: capi posix pid, Up: capi posix

9.2.6 Forking and executing processes

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_system (ikptr command)

Interface to the C function system(), system. Execute a command through the system shell; command must reference a bytevector object holding the command to execute. If successful return the termination status of the executed process, capi posix status for details; if an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_fork (void)

Interface to the C function fork(), fork. Create a new process by forking the current; if successful return a non–negative fixnum representing the the return value of fork(); if an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_execv (ikptr filename, ikptr argv)

Interface to the C function execv(), execv. filename must be a bytevector representing the pathname of an executable file; argv must be a list of bytevectors representing command line arguments. Execute the command; if the function returns: an error has occurred, return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_execve (ikptr filename, ikptr argv, ikptr env)

Interface to the C function execve(), execve. filename must be a bytevector representing the pathname of an executable file; argv must be a list of bytevectors representing command line arguments; env must be a list of bytevectors representing environment variables assignments. Execute the command; if the function returns: an error has occurred, return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_execvp (ikptr filename, ikptr argv)

Interface to the C function execvp(), execvp. filename must be a bytevector representing the file name of an executable file reachable in the current PATH; argv must be a list of bytevectors representing command line arguments. Execute the command; if the function returns: an error has occurred, return an encoded errno value.

Next: capi posix signals, Previous: capi posix process, Up: capi posix

9.2.7 Process termination status

The following functions accept as argument a fixnum representing the process termination status, for example the return value of system() or the status acquired by waitpid().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_waitpid (ikptr pid, ikptr options)

Interface to the C function waitpid(), waitpid. Request status informations on a process or group of processes knowing the identifier. If successful return a fixnum representing the status; if an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_wait (void)

Interface to the C function wait(), wait. Request status informations on any process or group of processes. If successful return a fixnum representing the status; if an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_WIFEXITED (ikptr status)

Interface to the C macro WIFEXITED(), WIFEXITED. Return true if the process terminated normally with exit().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_WEXITSTATUS (ikptr status)

Interface to the C macro WEXITSTATUS(), WEXITSTATUS. If WIFEXITED() applied to status would return true: return the low–order 8 bits from the exit status, which is the process exit status selected with exit().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_WIFSIGNALED (ikptr status)

Interface to the C macro WIFSIGNALED(), WIFSIGNALED. Return true if the process terminated because it received an interprocess signal which was not handled.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_WTERMSIG (ikptr status)

Interface to the C macro WTERMSIG(), WTERMSIG. If WIFSIGNALED() applied to status would return true: return the number of the interprocess signal that terminated the process.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_WCOREDUMP (ikptr status)

Interface to the C macro WCOREDUMP(), WCOREDUMP. Return true if the process terminated and produced a core dump.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_WIFSTOPPED (ikptr status)

Interface to the C macro WIFSTOPPED(), WIFSTOPPED. Return true if the process is stopped.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_WSTOPSIG (ikptr status)

Interface to the C macro WSTOPSIG(), WSTOPSIG. If WIFSTOPPED() applied to status would return true: return the number of the interprocess signal that caused the process to stop.

Next: capi posix stat, Previous: capi posix status, Up: capi posix

9.2.8 Delivering interprocess signals

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_raise (ikptr signum)

Interface to the C function raise(), raise. Send the selected signal to the calling process. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno code.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_kill (ikptr pid, ikptr signum)

Interface to the C function kill(), kill. Send the selected signal to selected process. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno code.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_pause (void)

Interface to the C function pause(), pause. Suspend the process until a signal is received. Return the void object.

Next: capi posix file, Previous: capi posix signals, Up: capi posix

9.2.9 File system inspection

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_stat (ikptr pathname, ikptr stat, ikpcb * pcb)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_lstat (ikptr pathname, ikptr stat, ikpcb * pcb)

Interfaces to the C functions stat() and lstat(), stat. Inspect the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector, and fill the struct-stat instance referenced by stat with the results. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_fstat (ikptr fd, ikptr stat, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function fstat(), fstat. Inspect the file system entry associated to the file descriptor fd, which must be a fixnum, and fill the struct-stat instance referenced by stat with the results. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_directory (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_char_device (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_block_device (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_regular_file (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_symbolic_link (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_socket (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_fifo (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_message_queue (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_semaphore (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_is_shared_memory (ikptr pathname, ikptr follow)

Return #t or #f whether the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector, is of the specified type; if an error occurs return an encoded errno value. When follow is true: stat() is used to inspect the entry, else lstat() is used.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_access (ikptr pathname, ikptr how)

Interface to the C function access(), access. Test the access mode selected by how, which must be a fixnum, for the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector. Return #t or #f or an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_size (ikptr filename, ikpcb * pcb)

Determine the size of the file selected by filename, which must be a bytevector, relying on a call to stat(). If successful: return an exact integer representing the size, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_atime (ikptr pathname, ikptr vector, ikpcb * pcb)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_mtime (ikptr pathname, ikptr vector, ikpcb * pcb)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_file_ctime (ikptr pathname, ikptr vector, ikpcb * pcb)

Compute an exact integer representing the access, modification and creation times for pathname, which must be a bytevector. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

The vector argument must be a vector which is mutated as follows: the first item holds an exact integer representing the number of seconds, the second item holds an exact integer representing the number of microseconds.

Next: capi posix link, Previous: capi posix stat, Up: capi posix

9.2.10 File system interface

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_chown (ikptr pathname, ikptr owner, ikptr group)

Interface to the C function chown(), chown. Changes the owner and group of the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector. owner and group must be fixnums. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_fchown (ikptr fd, ikptr owner, ikptr group)

Interface to the C function fchown(), fchown. Changes the owner and group of the file system entry selected by fd, which must be a fixnum representing a platform file descriptor. owner and group must be fixnums. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_chmod (ikptr pathname, ikptr mode)

Interface to the C function chmod(), chmod. Change to mode, which must be a fixnum, the access permissions for the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_fchmod (ikptr fd, ikptr mode)

Interface to the C function fchmod(), fchmod. Change to mode, which must be a fixnum, the access permissions for the file system entry associated to fd, which must be a fixnum representing a platform file descriptor. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_umask (ikptr mask)

Interface to the C function umask(), umask. Set the current file creation mask to mask which must be a fixnum and return the previous mask as a fixnum.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getumask (void)

Interface to the C function getumask(), getumask. Return the current file creation mask as a fixnum.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_utime (ikptr pathname, ikptr atime_sec, ikptr mtime_sec)

Interface to the C function utime(), utime. Set the access and modification times of the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector, to the specified counts of seconds; both atime_sec and mtime_sec must be fixnums. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_utimes (ikptr pathname, ikptr atime_sec, ikptr atime_usec, ikptr mtime_sec, ikptr mtime_usec)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_lutimes (ikptr pathname, ikptr atime_sec, ikptr atime_usec, ikptr mtime_sec, ikptr mtime_usec)

Interface to the C functions utimes() and lutimes(), utimes. Set the access and modification times of the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector, to the specified counts of seconds and microseconds; all the numeric arguments must be fixnums. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_futimes (ikptr fd, ikptr atime_sec, ikptr atime_usec, ikptr mtime_sec, ikptr mtime_usec)

Interface to the C function futimes(), futimes. Set the access and modification times of the file system entry associated to fd, which must be a fixnum representing a file descriptor, to the specified counts of seconds and microseconds; all the numeric arguments must be fixnums. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

Next: capi posix dir, Previous: capi posix file, Up: capi posix

9.2.11 Hard and symbolic links

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_link (ikptr old_pathname, ikptr new_pathname)

Interface to the C function link(), link. Create a hard link new_pathname to the source file system entry old_pathname. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_symlink (ikptr file_pathname, ikptr link_pathname)

Interface to the C function symlink(), symlink. Create a symbolic link link_pathname to the source file system entry file_pathname. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_readlink (ikptr link_pathname, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function readlink(), readlink. If pathname references a symbolic link: follow it once and return the referenced pathname as bytevector; if an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_realpath (ikptr pathname)

Interface to the C function realpath(), realpath. If pathname references a symbolic link: follow it and return the real pathname as bytevector; if an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_unlink (ikptr pathname)

Interface to the C function unlink(), unlink. Delete the file system entry referenced by pathname, which must be a bytevector and referencing a file. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_remove (ikptr pathname)

Interface to the C function remove(), remove. Delete the file system entry referenced by pathname, which must be a bytevector and referencing a file or directory. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_rename (ikptr old_pathname, ikptr new_pathname)

Interface to the C function rename(), rename. Rename the file system entry old_pathname to new_pathname, both of which must be bytevectors. If successful return zero, else return an encoded errno value.

Next: capi posix fd, Previous: capi posix link, Up: capi posix

9.2.12 File system directories

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_mkdir (ikptr pathname, ikptr mode)

Interface to the C function mkdir(), mkdir. Create a new directory file system entry with name pathname, which must be a bytevector; mode must be a fixnum specifying access permissions. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_rmdir (ikptr pathname)

Interface to the C function rmdir(), rmdir. Remove the directory file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getcwd (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getcwd(), getcwd. Acquire the pathname of the current working directory. If successful return a bytevector holding the pathname, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_chdir (ikptr pathname)

Interface to the C function chdir(), chdir. Change the current working directory to the file system entry selected by pathname, which must be a bytevector. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_fchdir (ikptr fd)

Interface to the C function fchdir(), fchdir. Change the current working directory to the file system entry associated to fd, which must be a fixnum representing a file descriptor. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_opendir (ikptr pathname, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function opendir(), opendir. Open a directory stream for the inspection of the file system entry pathname, which must be a bytevector. If successful return a pointer object, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_fdopendir (ikptr fd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function fdopendir(), fdopendir. Open a directory stream for the inspection of the file system entry associated to fd, which must be a fixnum representing a file descriptor. If successful return a pointer object, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_readdir (ikptr pointer, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function readdir(), readdir. Acquire the next entry from a directory stream referenced by pointer, which must be a pointer object. If successful and an entry is available: return a pointer object; if successful and no more entries are available: return the false object; else return an encoded errno value.

When no more entries are available or an error occurs: the directory stream is closed.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_closedir (ikptr pointer, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function closedir(), closedir. Close the directory stream referenced by pointer, which must be a pointer object. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_rewinddir (ikptr pointer)

Interface to the C function rewinddir(), rewinddir. Rewind to the beginning the directory stream referenced by pointer, which must be a pointer object. Return the void object.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_telldir (ikptr pointer)

Interface to the C function telldir(), telldir. Return an exact integer representing the current position in the directory stream referenced by pointer, which must be a pointer object.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_seekdir (ikptr pointer, ikptr pos)

Interface to the C function seekdir(), seekdir. Set to pos the position of the directory stream referenced by pointer, which must be a pointer object; pos must be the return value of a previous call to telldir(). Return the void object.

Next: capi posix socket, Previous: capi posix dir, Up: capi posix

9.2.13 File descriptors at low level

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_open (ikptr pathname, ikptr flags, ikptr mode)

Interface to the C function open(), open. Open a file descriptor for the file system entry pathname, which must be a bytevector; flags and mode must be fixnums. If successful return a fixnum representing the file descriptor, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_close (ikptr fd)

Interface to the C function close(), close. Close a file descriptor represented by fd, which must be a fixnum. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_read (ikptr fd, ikptr buffer, ikptr size)

Interface to the C function read(), read. Read bytes from the file descriptor fd and store them in the bytevector buffer; if size is a fixnum, read size bytes; if size is false, read a number of bytes equal to the length of buffer. If successful return a non–negative fixnum representing the number of bytes read, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_pread (ikptr fd, ikptr buffer, ikptr size, ikptr off)

Interface to the C function pread(), pread. Like ikrt_posix_read(), but start reading at offset off from the start of the file; off must be a non–negative exact integer.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_write (ikptr fd, ikptr buffer, ikptr size)

Interface to the C function write(), write. Write bytes to the file descriptor fd from the bytevector buffer; if size is a fixnum, write size bytes; if size is false, write a number of bytes equal to the length of buffer. If successful return a non–negative fixnum representing the number of written bytes, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_pwrite (ikptr fd, ikptr buffer, ikptr size, ikptr off)

Interface to the C function pwrite(), pwrite. Like ikrt_posix_write(), but start writing at offset off from the start of the file; off must be a non–negative exact integer.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_lseek (ikptr fd, ikptr off, ikptr whence, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function lseek(), lseek. Change the file position of the file descriptor fd to off from whence; fd and whence must be fixnums, off must be an exact integer. If successful return a non–negative exact integer representing the number of bytes from the beginning of the file, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_readv (ikptr fd, ikptr buffers, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function readv(), readv. Read bytes from the file descriptor fd and store them into the list of bytevectors referenced by buffers. If successful return a non–negative exact integer representing the number of bytes actually read, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_writev (ikptr fd, ikptr buffers, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function writev(), writev. Write bytes to the file descriptor fd from the list of bytevectors referenced by buffers. If successful return a non–negative exact integer representing the number of bytes actually written, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_select (ikptr nfds, ikptr read_fds, ikptr write_fds, ikptr except_fds, ikptr sec, ikptr usec, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function select(), select. Wait for read, write or exceptional events on selected lists of file descriptors.

nfds must be false or a non–negative fixnum, when false it defaults to the maximum file descriptor value in the given lists; it is the maximum file descriptor number in the sets to be checked for events, plus one. read_fds, write_fds and except_fds must be nil or lists of file descriptors to be checked for events. sec and usec must be fixnums representing timeout seconds and microseconds.

Return the fixnum zero if the timeout expired before any event arrived; else return a vector of 3 elements being lists of file descriptors, respectively, ready for reading, writing or an exceptional condition. If an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_select_fd (ikptr fd, ikptr sec, ikptr usec, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function select(), select. Wait for read, write or exceptional events on the single file descriptor fd. sec and usec must be fixnums representing timeout seconds and microseconds.

Return the fixnum zero if the timeout expired before any event arrived; else return a vector of 3 elements being false or fd, respectively, if fd is ready for reading, writing or an exceptional condition. If an error occurs: return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_fcntl (ikptr fd, ikptr command, ikptr arg)

Interface to the C function fcntl(), fcntl. Perform the operation specified by command on the file descriptor fd using arg; fd and command must be fixnums; arg must be the false object, a fixnum, a bytevector or a pointer, if it is #f no argument is handed to fcntl(). If successful return a fixnum representing the return value of fcntl(), else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_ioctl (ikptr fd, ikptr command, ikptr arg)

Interface to the C function ioctl(), ioctl. Perform the operation specified by command on the file descriptor fd using arg; fd and command must be fixnums; arg must be the false object, a fixnum, a bytevector or a pointer, if it is #f no argument is handed to ioctl(). If successful return a fixnum representing the return value of ioctl(), else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_dup (ikptr fd)

Interface to the C function dup(), dup. Duplicate the file descriptor fd. If successful return a non–negative fixnum representing the new descriptor, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_dup2 (ikptr old, ikptr new)

Interface to the C function dup2(), dup. Duplicate the file descriptor old to new. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_pipe (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function pipe(), pipe. Create a pair of file descriptors connected through a pipe. If successful return a pair whose car and cdr are fixnums representing the file descriptors, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_mkfifo (ikptr pathname, ikptr mode)

Interface to the C function mkfifo(), mkfifo. Create a FIFO special file with name pathname, which must be a bytevector, and mode mode, which must be a fixnum. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

Next: capi posix users, Previous: capi posix fd, Up: capi posix

9.2.14 Network sockets

Address structures
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_make_sockaddr_un (ikptr pathname, ikpcb * pcb)

Given a bytevector pathname representing the pathname of a local socket, build and return a bytevector holding the struct sockaddr_un representing it.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_sockaddr_un_pathname (ikptr socket_address, ikpcb * pcb)

Given a bytevector socket_address, which must be the return value of a previous call to ikrt_posix_make_sockaddr_un(), holding a struct sockaddr_un build and return a bytevector holding the corresponding socket pathname. If the data in socket_address is invalid: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_make_sockaddr_in (ikptr host_address, ikptr port, ikpcb * pcb)

Given a bytevector host_address holding a struct in_addr and a fixnum port representing a network port number, build and return a bytevector holding a struct sockaddr_in initialised with this data.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_sockaddr_in_in_addr (ikptr socket_address, ikpcb * pcb)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_sockaddr_in_in_port (ikptr socket_address)

Given a bytevector socket_address holding a struct sockaddr_in, extract the in_addr and in_port fields and return them as bytevector holding the corresponding struct in_addr and as fixnum. If the data in socket_address is invalid: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_make_sockaddr_in6 (ikptr host_address, ikptr port, ikpcb * pcb)

Given a bytevector host_address holding a struct in6_addr and a fixnum port representing a network port number, build and return a bytevector holding a struct sockaddr_in6 initialised with this data.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_sockaddr_in6_in6_addr (ikptr socket_address, ikpcb * pcb)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_sockaddr_in6_in6_port (ikptr socket_address)

Given a bytevector socket_address holding a struct sockaddr_in6, extract the in6_addr and in6_port fields and return them as bytevector holding the corresponding struct in6_addr and as fixnum. If the data in socket_address is invalid: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_in6addr_loopback (ikpcb * pcb)
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_in6addr_any (ikpcb * pcb)

Build and return a bytevector holding the constant structures of type struct in6_addr defined by in6addr_loopback and in6addr_any.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_inet_aton (ikptr dotted_quad, ikpcb * pcb)

Given the bytevector dotted_quad holding the ASCII dotted quad representation of a host address, build and return a bytevector holding the corresponding struct in_addr. If dotted_quad is invalid: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_inet_ntoa (ikptr host_address, ikpcb * pcb)

Given the bytevector host_address holding a struct in_addr, build and return a bytevector holding the corresponding ASCII dotted quad representation.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_inet_pton (ikptr af, ikptr presentation, ikpcb * pcb)

Given the fixnum af, being AF_INET or AF_INET6, and the bytevector presentation holding the ASCII presentation of an Internet address, build and return a bytevector holding the corresponding struct in_addr or struct in6_addr. If either af or presentation is invalid: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_inet_ntop (ikptr af, ikptr host_address, ikpcb * pcb)

Given the fixnum af, being AF_INET or AF_INET6, and the bytevector host_address holding a struct in_addr or struct in6_addr, build and return a bytevector holding the corresponding ASCII presentation of the Internet address . If the arguments are invalid: return false.

Host address resolution
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_gethostbyname (ikptr rtd, ikptr hostname, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function gethostbyname(), gethostbyname. Given the bytevector hostname holding the ASCII representation of a host name, build and return an instance of struct-hostent using rtd as its type descriptor. If an error occurs, return an encoded h_errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_gethostbyaddr (ikptr rtd, ikptr addr, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function gethostbyaddr(), gethostbyaddr. Given the bytevector addr holding a struct in_addr or a struct in6_addr, build and return an instance of struct-hostent using rtd as its type descriptor; the type of address is automatically inferred from the length of the bytevector. If an error occurs, return an encoded h_errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_host_entries (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C functions sethostent(), gethostent() and endhostent(), gethostbyaddr. Build and return a list of struct-hostent representing the entries in the hosts database, using rtd as type descriptor.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getaddrinfo (ikptr rtd, ikptr node, ikptr service, ikptr hints, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getaddrinfo(), see the manual page getaddrinfo(3). Given the bytevectors node and service identifying an Internet host and a service, build a list of struct-addrinfo instances representing addresses to which sockets can be bound or connected.

Both node and service can be false, in which case the corresponding arguments handed to the C function are NULL.

hints must be an instance of struct-addrinfo used to select matching hosts. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-addrinfo.

If successful: return the list of data structures, else return a fixnum representing an EAI_ error code.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_gai_strerror (ikptr error_code, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function gai_strerror(), see the manual page gai_strerror(3). Convert a EAI_ error code into the corresponding error message, return a bytevector holding such message in ASCII coding.

Network protocols
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getprotobyname (ikptr rtd, ikptr name, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getprotobyname(), getprotobyname. Given a bytevector name holding the ASCII coding of a network protocol name, query the network protocols database and build an instance of struct-protoent mirroring the resulting struct protoent entry; rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-protoent. If successful return the data structure, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getprotobynumber (ikptr rtd, ikptr proto_num, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getprotobynumber(), getprotobynumber. Given a fixnum proto_num being the number of a network protocol, query the network protocols database and build an instance of struct-protoent mirroring the resulting struct protoent entry; rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-protoent. If successful return the data structure, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_protocol_entries (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C functions setprotoent(), getprotoent() and endprotoent(), setprotoent. Scan the network protocol database and build a list of struct-protoent mirroring the resulting struct protoent entries; rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-protoent. Return the list of structures.

Network services
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getservbyname (ikptr rtd, ikptr name, ikptr protocol, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getservbyname(), getservbyname. Given the bytevectors name and protocol holding the ASCII coding of a network service name and protocol, query the network services database and build an instance of struct-servent mirroring the resulting struct servent entry. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-servent. If successful return the data structure, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getservbynumber (ikptr rtd, ikptr port, ikptr protocol, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getservbynumber(), getservbynumber. Given a fixnum port and a string or bytevector protocol being the port number and protocol name of a network service, query the network services database and build an instance of struct-servent mirroring the resulting struct servent entry. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-servent. If successful return the data structure, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_service_entries (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C functions setservent(), getservent() and endservent(), setservent. Scan the network service database and build a list of struct-servent mirroring the resulting struct servent entries. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-servent. Return the list of structures.

Networks database
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getnetbyname (ikptr rtd, ikptr name, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getnetbyname(), getnetbyname. Given the bytevector name holding the ASCII coding of a network name, query the networks database and build an instance of struct-netent mirroring the resulting struct netent entry. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-netent. If successful return the data structure, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getnetbyaddr (ikptr rtd, ikptr net, ikptr type, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getnetbyaddr(), getnetbyaddr. Given an exact integer net representing a network number and the fixnum type representing a network type, query the networks database and build an instance of struct-netent mirroring the resulting struct netent entry. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-netent. If successful return the data structure, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_network_entries (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C functions setnetent(), getnetent() and endnetent(), setnetent. Scan the networks database and build a list of struct-netent mirroring the resulting struct netent entries. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-netent. Return the list of structures.

Sockets creation and shutdown
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_socket (ikptr namespace, ikptr style, ikptr protocol)

Interface to the C function socket(), socket. Create a new socket descriptor and return it as non–negative fixnum; if an error occurs return an encoded errno value. All the arguments must be fixnums.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_shutdown (ikptr sock, ikptr how)

Interface to the C function shutdown(), shutdown. Close the socket sock according to how. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_socketpair (ikptr namespace, ikptr style, ikptr protocol, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function socketpair(), socketpair. Create a pairs of connected sockets and return a pair holding the descriptors as non–negative fixnums; if an error occurs return an encoded errno value. All the arguments must be fixnums, but pcb.

Socket operations
— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_connect (ikptr sock, ikptr addr)

Interface to the C function connect(), connect. Connect the socket sock to the address specified by the bytevector addr which must hold a concrete instance of struct sockaddr. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_listen (ikptr sock, ikptr pending_conns)

Interface to the C function listen(), listen. Enable the socket sock to accept connections; the fixnum pending_conns specifies the maximum length of the pending connection requests queue. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_accept (ikptr sock, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function accept(), accept. Accept an incoming connection to the server socket sock. If successful return a pair whose car is a non–negative fixnum representing the socket and whose cdr is a bytevector representing the client address as struct sockaddr; else return an encoded errno value, including EWOULDBLOCK which means that sock is in non–blocking mode and no pending connections exist.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_bind (ikptr sock, ikptr sockaddr)

Interface to the C function bind(), bind. Bind the socket descriptor sock to the address specified by the struct sockaddr in the bytevector sockaddr. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getpeername (ikptr sock, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getpeername(), getpeername. Retrieve informations about the address of the socket to which the sock socket is connected to. If successful return a bytevector holding a struct sockaddr, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getsockname (ikptr sock, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getsockanme(), getsockname. Retrieve informations about the address bound to the socket descriptor sock. If successful return a bytevector holding the struct sockaddr, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_send (ikptr sock, ikptr buffer, ikptr size, ikptr flags)

Interface to the C function send(), send. Like write() but with the additional argument flags which must be a fixnum: write data from the bytevector buffer to the socket sock; if size is a fixnum, write size bytes; if size is false, write a number of bytes equal to the length of buffer. If successful return a non–negative fixnum representing the number of bytes actually sent, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_recv (ikptr sock, ikptr buffer, ikptr size, ikptr flags)

Interface to the C function recv(), recv. Like read() but with the additional argument flags which must be a fixnum: read data from sock and store it in the bytevector buffer; if size is a fixnum, read size bytes; if size is false, read a number of bytes equal to the length of buffer. If successful return a non–negative fixnum representing the number of bytes actually received, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_sendto (ikptr sock, ikptr buffer, ikptr size, ikptr flags, ikptr addr)

Interface to the C function sendto(), sendto. Like send() but with the additional argument addr which must be a bytevector holding a struct sockaddr: write data from the bytevector buffer to the socket sock to the destination specified by addr.

If size is a fixnum, write size bytes; if size is false, write a number of bytes equal to the length of buffer.

If successful return a non–negative fixnum representing the number of bytes actually sent, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_recvfrom (ikptr sock, ikptr buffer, ikptr size, ikptr flags, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function recvfrom(), recvfrom. Like recv() but additionally retrieve informations about the address of the sender: read data from sock and store it in the bytevector buffer.

If size is a fixnum, read size bytes; if size is false, read a number of bytes equal to the length of buffer.

If successful return a pair whose car is a non–negative fixnum representing the number of bytes actually received and whose cdr is a bytevector holding a struct sockaddr representing the address of the sender; else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getsockopt (ikptr sock, ikptr level, ikptr option, ikptr optval, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getsockopt(), getsockopt. Retrieve the value of option of socket sock at level and store it in the bytevector optval. option and level must be fixnums. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setsockopt (ikptr sock, ikptr level, ikptr option, ikptr optval, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function setsockopt(), setsockopt. Set a new value for option of socket sock at level reading it from the bytevector optval. option and level must be fixnums. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

Next: capi posix job, Previous: capi posix socket, Up: capi posix

9.2.15 Users and groups

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getuid (void)

Interface to the C function getuid(), getuid. Return a fixnum representing the real user ID of the process.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getgid (void)

Interface to the C function getgid(), getgid. Return a fixnum representing the real group ID of the process.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_geteuid (void)

Interface to the C function geteuid(), geteuid. Return a fixnum representing the effective user ID of the process.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getegid (void)

Interface to the C function getegid(), getegid. Return a fixnum representing the effective group ID of the process.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getgroups (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getgroups(), getgroups. Return a list of fixnums representing the supplementary group IDs of the process; if an error occurs return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_seteuid (ikptr new_uid)

Interface to the C function seteuid(), seteuid. Set the effective user ID to new_uid, which must be a fixnum. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setuid (ikptr new_uid)

Interface to the C function setuid(), setuid. Set both the real and effective user IDs to new_uid, which must be a fixnum. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setreuid (ikptr real_uid, ikptr effective_uid)

Interface to the C function setreuid(), setreuid. Set the real user ID to real_uid and the effective user ID to effective_uid, both the arguments must be fixnums. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setegid (ikptr new_gid)

Interface to the C function setegid(), setegid. Set the effective group ID to new_gid, which must be a fixnum. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setgid (ikptr new_gid)

Interface to the C function setgid(), setgid. Set both the real and effective group IDs to new_gid, which must be a fixnum. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setregid (ikptr real_gid, ikptr effective_gid)

Interface to the C function setregid(), setregid. Set the real group ID to real_gid and the effective group ID to effective_gid, both the arguments must be fixnums. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getlogin (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getlogin(), getlogin. Return a bytevector holding the ASCII coding of the name of the user logged in on the controlling terminal of the process; if the name cannot be determined: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getpwuid (ikptr rtd, ikptr uid, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getpwuid(), getpwuid. Retrieve informations on the user with identifier uid, which must be a fixnum. If successful return an instance of struct-passwd initialised with rtd, which must be its type descriptor; if a user with such an ID does not exists: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getpwnam (ikptr rtd, ikptr name, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getpwnam(), getpwnam. Retrieve informations on the user with name represented in ASCII coding by the bytevector name. If successful return an instance of struct-passwd initialised with rtd, which must be its type descriptor; if a user with such an ID does not exists: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_user_entries (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C functions setpwent(), getpwent() and endpwent(), setpwent. Iterate the database of users and return a list of struct-passwd representing the entries; the structures are initialised with rtd which must be the type descriptor of struct-passwd.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getgrgid (ikptr rtd, ikptr gid, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getgrgid(), getgrgid. Retrieve informations on the group with identifier gid, which must be a fixnum. If successful return an instance of struct-group initialised with rtd, which must be its type descriptor; if a group with such an ID does not exists: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getgrnam (ikptr rtd, ikptr name, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function getgrnam(), getgrnam. Retrieve informations on the group with name represented in ASCII coding by the bytevector name. If successful return an instance of struct-group initialised with rtd, which must be its type descriptor; if a group with such an ID does not exists: return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_group_entries (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C functions setgrent(), getgrent() and endgrent(), setgrent. Iterate the database of groups and return a list of struct-group representing the entries; the structures are initialised with rtd which must be the type descriptor of struct-group.

Next: capi posix time, Previous: capi posix users, Up: capi posix

9.2.16 Job control

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_ctermid (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function ctermid(), ctermid. Return a bytevector holding the ASCII coded pathname of the controlling terminal of the current process; the returned value may be the empty bytevector.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setsid (void)

Interface to the C function setsid(), setsid. Create a new session, making the current process the group leader with no controlling terminal. If successful return a fixnum representing the new process groups ID, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getsid (ikptr pid)

Interface to the C function getsid(), getsid. If successful return a fixnum representing the session ID of the process with process ID pid, which must be a fixnum; else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_getpgrp (void)

Interface to the C function getpgrp(), getpgrp. Return a fixnum representing the process group ID of the calling process.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_setpgid (ikptr pid, ikptr pgid)

Interface to the C function setpgid(), setpgid. Put the process pid in the process group pgid. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_tcgetpgrp (ikptr fd)

Interface to the C function tcgetpgrp(), tcgetpgrp. If successful return a fixnum representing the process group ID of the foreground process group associated with the terminal open on descriptor fd, which must be a fixnum; else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_tcsetpgrp (ikptr fd, ikptr pgid)

Interface to the C function tcsetpgrp(), tcsetpgrp. Set to process group ID pgid the foreground process group for the terminal open on descriptor fd; both the arguments must be fixnums. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_tcgetsid (ikptr fd)

Interface to the C function tcgetsid(), tcgetsid. If successful return a fixnum representing the process group ID of the session for which the terminal open on descriptor fd is the controlling terminal; else return an encoded errno value.

Previous: capi posix job, Up: capi posix

9.2.17 Date and time

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_clock (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function clock(), clock. If successful return an inexact integer representing the CPU time for the calling process expressed in clock ticks; if the clock time is not available return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_times (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function times(), times. If successful return an instance of struct-tms representing the current processor time with all the fields set to inexact integers, else return false; rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-tms.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_time (ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function time(), time. If successful return the calendar time as an inexact integer, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_gettimeofday (ikptr rtd, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function gettimeofday(), gettimeofday. Acquire the current time. If successful return an instance of struct-timeval, else return an encoded errno value. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-timeval.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_localtime (ikptr rtd, ikptr time, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function localtime(), localtime. Given an exact integer time representing the local time as returned by the posix-time function: build and return an instance of struct-tm representing the same time in human readable form; if an error occurs return false. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-tm.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_gmtime (ikptr rtd, ikptr time, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function gmtime(), gmtime. Given an exact integer time representing the UTC time as returned by the posix-time function: build and return an instance of struct-tm representing the same time in human readable form; if an error occurs return false. rtd must be the type descriptor of struct-tm.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_timelocal (ikptr tm, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function timelocal(), timelocal. Given a reference to a struct-rm, tm, representing a local broken time, convert it into a time value as returned by time(). If successful return an inexact integer representing the time value, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_timegm (ikptr tm, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function timegm(), timegm. Given a reference to a struct-rm, tm, representing a UTC broken time, convert it into a time value as returned by time(). If successful return an inexact integer representing the time value, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_posix_strftime (ikptr template, ikptr tm, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function strftime(), strftime. Given a bytevector template holding an ASCII coded format string and a struct-tm instance tm: build a formatted time string; the resulting time string can be at most 4096 bytes wide. If successful return a bytevector holding the time string in ASCII coding, else return false.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_nanosleep (ikptr secs, ikptr nsecs)

Interface to the C function nanosleep(), nanosleep. Halt the current process for the specified amount of time.

The count of seconds secs must be an exact integer in the range [0, 2^32); the count of nanoseconds nsecs must be an exact integer in the range [0, 999999999].

If successful and the requested time is elapsed: return a pair whose car is false and whose cdr is false. If successful and the sleeping was interrupted by an interprocess signal: return a pair whose car is an exact integer representing the count of remaining seconds and whose cdr is an exact integer representing the count of remaining nanoseconds. If an error occurs return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_current_time (ikptr time)

Interface to the gettimeofday() C function. gettimeofday. Retrieve the current time. time must reference a time internal structure, which is filled with three values: megaseconds, seconds and microseconds. Always return time itself.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_gmt_offset (ikptr time)

Compute the offset in seconds between the local time and the UTC time. time must reference a time internal structure, already filled with megaseconds, seconds and microseconds. Return a fixnum representing the offset.

Next: capi glibc, Previous: capi posix, Up: capi

9.3 C language level GNU+Linux interface

  • capi linux status: Process termination status.

Up: capi linux

9.3.1 Process termination status

— Function: ikptr ikrt_linux_waitid (ikptr idtype, ikptr id, ikptr info, ikptr options)

Interface to the Linux specific C function waitid(), see the waitid() manual page for details. Wait for the termination of one or more child processes with finer control of waitpid(). The arguments idtype, id and options must be fixnums. info must be a reference to a structure of type struct-siginfo_t, linux status for details. If successful: return info itself, else raise an exception.

The following functions accept as argument a fixnum representing the process termination status, for example the return value of system() or the status acquired by waitpid().

— Function: ikptr ikrt_linux_WIFCONTINUED (ikptr status)

Interface to the Linux specific C macro WIFCONTINUED(). Return true if the process was resumed by delivery of SIGCONT.

Interface to the C function clearenv(), clearenv. Remove all the entries from the environment. Return the void object.

9.4.2 File system directories

— Function: ikptr ikrt_glibc_dirfd (ikptr pointer)

Interface to the C function dirfd(), dirfd. Acquire a file descriptor associated to the directory entry referenced by pointer, which must be a pointer object to a directory entry. If successful return a fixnum representing the file descriptor, else return an encoded errno value.

9.4.3 Temporary files and directories

— Function: ikptr ikrt_glibc_mkstemp (ikptr template, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function mkstemp(), mkstemp. Create a temporary file, open it and open a file descriptor for reading and writing. template must be a mutable bytevector holding a template pathname on entering and the actual pathname on returning. If successful return a file descriptor, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_glibc_mkdtemp (ikptr template, ikpcb * pcb)

Interface to the C function mkdtemp(), mkdtemp. Create a temporary directory for reading and writing. template must be a mutable bytevector holding a template pathname on entering and the actual pathname on returning. If successful return template itself, else return an encoded errno value.

9.4.4 File system synchronisation

— Function: ikptr ikrt_glibc_sync (void)

Interface to the C function sync(), Synchronizing I/O. Flush kernel buffer data and meta informations to the file system devices. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_glibc_fsync (ikptr fd)

Interface to the C function fsync(), Synchronizing I/O. Flush kernel buffer data and meta informations to the file system device for the file descriptor fd. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.

— Function: ikptr ikrt_glibc_fdatasync (ikptr fd)

Interface to the C function fdatasync(), Synchronizing I/O. Flush kernel buffer data to the file system device for the file descriptor fd. If successful return the fixnum zero, else return an encoded errno value.
